has first suspected case of the coronavirus **29;42379;TOOLONG &lt;/ul&gt; &lt;p&gt; &lt;a href= " **26;42410;TOOLONG " **33;42438;TOOLONG &lt;/p&gt; Andy RigaThu , 23 Jan 2020 18:04:03 **45;42473;TOOLONG .
NewsNewsOpinion : Impending fertility crisis requires urgent actionhttp : **34;42520;TOOLONG .
&lt;img src= " https : **33;42556;TOOLONG .
title= " A container holding racks of frozen oocytes , or immature egg cells , are shown being pulled up from a liquid nitrogen storage tank at the NYU Fertility Center in New York , U .
, on May 1 , 2007 .
" As a consequence of rising rates of infertility , the number of couples seeking assisted reproductive treatment in western countries is increasing annually at a rate of 5 per cent , " Sarah Kimmins and Jo ? l Roy write .
" alt= " A container holding racks of frozen oocytes , or immature egg cells , are shown being pulled up from a liquid nitrogen storage tank at the NYU Fertility Center in New York , U .
, on May 1 , 2007 .
" As a consequence of rising rates of infertility , the number of couples seeking assisted reproductive treatment in western countries is increasing annually at a rate of 5 per cent , " Sarah Kimmins and Jo ? l Roy write .
" data-portal-copyright= " Lou Manna " **28;42591;TOOLONG " 1 " data-license-id= " 1701072 " /&gt; &lt;p&gt; Ask most men whether they are concerned about their ability to have children and the answer will be a resounding no .
Yet they should be concerned , now more than ever .
World-wide sperm counts have declined to less than half of what they were 40 years ago , and the number of abnormal sperm has doubled .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Despite headlines about the labour shortage and aging population , people remain strangely unaware of this impending fertility crisis .
As well , infertility is wrongly perceived as a female-only health issue .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; As a consequence of rising rates of infertility , the number of couples seeking assisted reproductive treatment in western countries is increasing annually at a rate of 5 per cent .
This is good news for the highly profitable fertility industry , but not for those who want to start a family .
In Canada , one in six couples experience infertility .
On average , they will spend $30,000 on treatments .
Few can afford such expensive procedures without incurring massive debt , and existing tax incentives do little to alleviate this burden .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; It&amp;rsquo ; s urgent that we move to ensure fair and equitable access to fertility treatment .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Article 3(a) of the Quebec Health Insurance Act provides that the cost of physicians&amp;rsquo ; services qualifying as &amp;ldquo ; medically required&amp;rdquo ; is covered by the RAMQ .
In 2015 , an amendment to the act voted under the Couillard government uninsured most assisted reproductive treatments in order to &amp;ldquo ; optimize the use of medical and financial resources .
&amp;rdquo ; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Male and female infertility is a disease .
It is recognized as such by the World Health Organization , among others .
Fertility treatments and assisted reproductive treatment therefore need to be understood as medically required .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Yet , existing rules create a regime that is incoherent .
For example , male fertility-restoring procedures such as varicocelectomy are fully covered by the public regime , as is the excision of ovarian cysts , a frequent cause of female infertility .
But &lt;span class= " s1 " &gt;many couples with other issues will find themselves needing to pay out of pocket for such treatments as in vitro fertilization .
&lt;/span&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Also worthy of mention is infertility&amp;rsquo ; s effect as a catalyst for such other afflictions as sexual dysfunction , depression and anxiety .
Ironically , these effects will be treated with full RAMQ support , potentially at a higher lifetime cost than fertility treatments would incur .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Quebec&amp;rsquo ; s exclusion of assisted reproductive treatment coverage also challenges the basic human right to family life , which is recognized in a variety of international instruments , including the Universal Declaration of Human Rights .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Also worth considering in terms of human rights is the unfair health burden placed on women for the treatment of infertility .
&lt;span class= " s1 " &gt;Despite male factors contributing to about half of cases , the diagnosis and treatment of infertility in men is based on old , ineffective methods .
As a consequence , only 4 per cent of infertile men can be diagnosed accurately .
Further , there are few fertility treatments for men .
As a consequence , it is usually the woman who must undergo treatment .
&lt;/span&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; This treatment of women for male infertility comes with increased health risks due to hormonal injections and oocyte ( egg ) retrieval , such as strokes and a possibly heightened risk of cancer .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; The remedy is to prioritize funding for research around the causes and treatment of male infertility , and to launch a public health campaign to inform men how lifestyle ( excess weight , poor diet , alcohol and/or cannabis consumption ) can harm fertility .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; It is time for our leaders to address this impending fertility crisis , and re-examine assisted reproductive treatment coverage from both an ethical and legal perspective .
Otherwise , we might soon live in a world where having a family becomes limited to top income earners , and where women have to pay the price of an increasingly male-centric issue .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &lt;em&gt;Sarah Kimmins is associate professor , reproductive biology at McGill University and Canada Research Chair Tier II , Epigenetics , Reproduction and Development , Centre for Research in Reproduction and Development .
Jo ? l Roy is a Montreal attorney practising in health law &lt;/em&gt; &lt;span class= " s1 " &gt;&lt;i&gt;with MERCIER LEDUC LLP .
&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt; &lt;/p&gt; Sarah Kimmins , Special to Montreal Gazette , Jo ? l Roy , Special to Montreal GazetteTue , 21 Jan 2020 18:51:08 **45;42621;TOOLONG .
Is it worth feeling the burn of HIIT ? http : **35;42668;TOOLONG .
&lt;img src= " https : **33;42705;TOOLONG .
title= " There are many formats for HIIT workouts , and no single one has been proved to provide the greatest return .
Some are performed on a treadmill , some on a stationary bike .
Some require 80 per cent of maximum effort , others demand close to 100 per cent .
" alt= " There are many formats for HIIT workouts , and no single one has been proved to provide the greatest return .
Some are performed on a treadmill , some on a stationary bike .
Some require 80 per cent of maximum effort , others demand close to 100 per cent .
" data-portal-copyright= " Allen McInnis " **28;42740;TOOLONG " 1 " data-license-id= " 1695775 " /&gt; &lt;iframe width= " 100% " height= " 100% " frameborder= " 0 " allowfullscreen= " true " src= " https : **34;42770;TOOLONG .
&gt; &lt;/iframe&gt; &lt;p&gt; Like many trendy workouts before it , high-intensity interval training ( HIIT ) has gone from being the next best thing to the greatest thing of all time .
This elevation in status from cool new workout to a workout that does everything for everyone is typical of most exercise fads that take the fitness world by storm .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; With HIIT voted No .
2 out of the top 20 fitness trends for 2020 by the American College of Sports Medicine , more and more people are jumping on the bandwagon , and more and more fitness clubs are offering HIIT workouts .
Yet despite all the hype , consider this a gentle reminder that no one workout does it all .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; What&amp;rsquo ; s the appeal of HIIT ? For today&amp;rsquo ; s time-crunched exerciser , it&amp;rsquo ; s the efficiency of the workouts .
Traditional workouts last anywhere from 30 to 60 minutes , whereas HIIT sessions last 10 minutes or less .
Best of all , those 10 minutes pack a mean punch , offering similar fitness and health gains as workouts that take twice as long ( or more ) .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; To reap those gains , you have to exercise at your maximum effort , albeit for short periods of time ( 60 to 240 seconds ) .
While there are myriad interval formats , HIIT results are based on repeated bouts of exercise performed anywhere from 80 to 100 per cent of all-out effort interspersed with periods of recovery .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; As long as exercisers consistently push themselves into that discomfort zone , research suggests HIIT workouts have the potential to significantly improve cardiorespiratory fitness and deliver all the health benefits that go along with it .
Keep in mind , however , most of the research protocols supporting the benefits of HIIT were performed in a lab , which doesn&amp;rsquo ; t always compare to the type of HIIT workouts offered at fitness clubs or online .
Not to mention that what works on one section of the population may not have the same effect on another .
So not all research results should be taken at face value .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Part of the reason it&amp;rsquo ; s so difficult to translate HIIT results from a research lab to real life is that there are so many workout formats , and no single one has been proved to provide the greatest return .
Some workouts are performed on a stationary bike and some are done on a treadmill .
Some require maintaining 80 per cent of maximum effort , while others demand exercisers push closer to 100 per cent .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Despite all the debate surrounding the benefits of HIIT , it&amp;rsquo ; s clear there&amp;rsquo ; s one promise that&amp;rsquo ; s continually oversold : HIIT isn&amp;rsquo ; t a magic bullet for losing unwanted weight or body fat .
A recent published review of 47 studies featuring 1,422 middle-aged and overweight individuals suggests that anyone who&amp;rsquo ; s sweating through HIIT sessions in the hope of losing a few pounds is likely to be disappointed .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;ldquo ; Our results revealed no evidence to suggest low-volume HIIT was beneficial for improvements in total body fat mass , body fat and lean body mass when compared to a non-exercising control or moderate intensity continuous training , &amp;rdquo ; said the Australian researchers who analyzed the available data .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; It&amp;rsquo ; s likely that what makes HIIT so popular is also what prevents it from affecting body weight and body composition .
Successful weight loss starts with workouts longer than 60 minutes , which far exceeds the characteristics of HIIT .
As for the ballyhooed afterburn of HIIT workouts , any extra calories burned post-exercise are unlikely to be significant enough to have an effect on weight loss .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; What does this mean for those who have switched from longer , steady-state workouts to HIIT ? It depends on your goals .
If you want an express workout that&amp;rsquo ; s guaranteed to improve your health and fitness , HIIT workouts are the way to go .
But if weight loss is your goal , you need far more minutes than what HIIT has to offer before you can buckle that belt a little tighter .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Also worth keeping in mind is that the majority of HIIT studies feature aerobic-type workouts &amp;mdash ; primarily cycling and running .
Most HIIT workouts offered in fitness studios or on YouTube feature a mix of aerobic and **32;42806;TOOLONG intervals , so the results may not mirror those published in research journals .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; No workout checks all the boxes .
But when it comes to improving overall fitness , nothing gets the job done in less time than HIIT .
That said , exercising at the top end of the effort scale isn&amp;rsquo ; t for everyone , so if feeling the burn isn&amp;rsquo ; t your thing , then trendy or not , HIIT&amp;rsquo ; s not for you .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;h2 class= " cat-head short " **40;42840;TOOLONG .
&lt;ul class= " relatedlinks " &gt; &lt;li&gt;&lt;a href= " https : **33;42882;TOOLONG .
healthy -- and well-timed -- diet fuels muscles of master **29;42917;TOOLONG &lt;li&gt;&lt;a href= " https : **33;42948;TOOLONG .
stretching a waste of time ? &lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt;&lt;a href= " https : **33;42983;TOOLONG .
from Jill **27;43018;TOOLONG &lt;/ul&gt; Jill Barker , Special to Montreal GazetteMon , 20 Jan 2020 20:06:21 **45;43047;TOOLONG &amp;amp ; FitnessHealthLifeLocal NewsChristopher Labos : One more reason to reduce your alcohol consumptionhttp : **29;43094;TOOLONG .
&lt;img src= " https : **33;43125;TOOLONG .
title= " " The idea of one or two drinks per day being good for you persists , despite the mounting evidence against it , " Christopher Labos writes .
" alt= " " The idea of one or two drinks per day being good for you persists , despite the mounting evidence against it , " Christopher Labos writes .
" data-portal-copyright= " PIERRE ANDRIEU " **28;43160;TOOLONG " 1 " data-license-id= " 1695162 " /&gt; &lt;p&gt; Everyone seems to think , or at least wants to believe , that alcohol in moderation is good for you .
But alcohol increases the risk of cancer , especially &lt;a href= " https : **33;43190;TOOLONG .
cancer&lt;/a&gt; , and the evidence for the supposed cardiovascular benefits of red wine is &lt;a href= " https : **33;43225;TOOLONG .
that great , &lt;/a&gt; either .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Alcohol , in fact , can be quite problematic .
It raises your &lt;a href= " https : **33;43260;TOOLONG .
target= " blank " rel= " noopener " &gt;blood pressure&lt;/a&gt; and the high sugar content contributes to &lt;a href= " https : **33;43295;TOOLONG .
target= " blank " rel= " noopener " &gt;weight gain&lt;/a&gt; .
As Tommy Schnurmacher has noted , there is a reason we call it a beer belly and not a celery belly .
Also , alcohol itself is toxic to heart muscle cells and can cause heart failure , although the condition , known as alcoholic cardiomyopathy , generally only happens when people drink heavily on a regular basis .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Still , the idea of one or two drinks per day being good for you persists , despite the mounting evidence against it .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; A new study in the &lt;a href= " https : **33;43330;TOOLONG .
target= " blank " rel= " noopener " &gt;New England Journal of Medicine&lt;/a&gt; looked at the effects of alcohol consumption and a type of arrhythmia known as atrial fibrillation ( or Afib ) .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Afib is a common arrhythmia that becomes more common as we age .
Interestingly , it often produces no symptoms and its major complication is not cardiac , but neurological .
Afib increases the risk of stroke , and patients often need to be prescribed blood thinners to try to prevent that .
Still , some people , especially younger patients , do feel palpitations when they have an irregular heartbeat .
Medications can control the arrhythmia , but some lifestyle factors can help , too .
Although age is a significant risk factor for developing Afib , obesity , hypertension , diabetes , sleep apnea and a sedentary lifestyle are all &lt;a href= " https : **33;43365;TOOLONG .
target= " blank " rel= " noopener " &gt;risk factors , &lt;/a&gt; as well .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Another risk factor that isn&amp;rsquo ; t always discussed is &lt;a href= " https : **33;43400;TOOLONG .
target= " blank " rel= " noopener " &gt;alcohol&lt;/a&gt; .
It increases the risk of Afib long-term and also can serve as a &lt;a href= " https : **33;43435;TOOLONG .
target= " blank " rel= " noopener " &gt;trigger&lt;/a&gt; for individual episodes .
How it does this is debatable .
Given that alcohol causes weight gain , high blood pressure and raises blood sugar , it is possible it is simply acting via these traditional cardiac risk factors .
But there is also evidence that alcohol can disrupt the electrical activity in the heart muscle and affect the heart muscle directly in the long term .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; While it has been clear for some time that lifestyle modifications like exercising more and eating healthily can help reduce Afib , the evidence concerning alcohol consumption has been less clear .
This new study tested whether abstinence prevented episodes of the arrhythmia .
In the study , 140 patients who drank on average 16-17 drinks per week were randomized to either give up alcohol entirely or continue as they were .
At six months , the Afib recurrence rate in the abstinence group was lower ( 53 per cent vs .
73 per cent ) as was the hospitalization rate ( 9 per cent vs .
20 per cent ) and the time between arrhythmia episodes was more spread out .
There also a 3 .
kg difference in weight and seven-point difference in blood pressure .
In short , cutting out alcohol helped tremendously .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; To be fair , at 17 drinks per week , the patients&amp;rsquo ; alcohol consumption was on the high side and whether someone who drank a more modest seven drinks per week would benefit to the same degree is up for debate .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Also , not everyone in the abstinence group completely gave up alcohol .
Around 40 per cent of them still drank some alcohol though most drank fewer than two drinks per week .
Still , this suggests that completely cutting out alcohol might not be necessary and that cutting back may accomplish quite a bit .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; The authors of the study acknowledged that alcohol is ingrained in Western culture .
Getting people to give it up entirely is almost certainly impractical .
But it might be worth remembering that alcohol is not so good for your heart .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; In fact , the strongest health benefits involving alcohol seem to be from drinking less of it .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &lt;em&gt;Christopher Labos&lt;/em&gt; &lt;em&gt; is a Montreal doctor and an associate with the McGill Office for Science and Society .
He also co-hosts a podcast called The Body of Evidence .
&lt;/em&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;h2 class= " cat-head short " **40;43470;TOOLONG .
&lt;ul class= " relatedlinks " &gt; &lt;li&gt;&lt;a href= " https : **33;43512;TOOLONG .
columns by Christopher **26;43547;TOOLONG &lt;/ul&gt; Christopher Labos , Special to Montreal GazetteTue , 14 Jan 2020 15:56:09 **45;43575;TOOLONG .
&amp;amp ; FitnessOpinionFitness : A healthy -- and well-timed -- diet fuels muscles of master athleteshttp : **32;43622;TOOLONG .
&lt;img src= " https : **33;43656;TOOLONG .
title= " One study of master athletes noted a 33- to 38-per-cent increase in muscle mass and strength among those who consistently consumed a high-protein post-weight-training snack compared to those who didn't .
" alt= " One study of master athletes noted a 33- to 38-per-cent increase in muscle mass and strength among those who consistently consumed a high-protein post-weight-training snack compared to those who didn't .
" data-portal-copyright= " Dave Sidaway " **28;43691;TOOLONG " 1 " data-license-id= " 1689510 " /&gt; &lt;p&gt; The last decade has seen a steep increase in the number of athletes achieving personal bests in their 40s and beyond .
This group of dedicated older athletes has redefined the idea of aging , rewriting the record books with performances in the pool , on the track , and in the saddle .
So remarkable are their achievements , exercise scientists have been busy studying their training and lifestyle habits to see if they can gather more information on what successful aging looks like .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; According to a group of French researchers , &lt;span class= " s1 " &gt;there is still a dearth of published research on the link between nutrition and performance in master athletes&lt;/span&gt; .
In particular , do older athletes have a different set of nutritional needs than their younger counterparts ? &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;ldquo ; We proposed to identify the metabolic challenges that master athletes may face and that require specific nutritional recommendations , &amp;rdquo ; said the French researchers in their article &lt;a href= " https : **33;43721;TOOLONG .
for Master Athletes : Is There a Need for Specific **25;43756;TOOLONG .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; One of the primary nutritional goals of any athlete is to adequately fuel training and performance .
Active individuals who engage in a high volume of exercise need to consume more calories than someone who is sedentary , based on a greater number of calories expended while training and competing .
But nutritional strategies for athletes go far beyond counting calories .
Knowing when to eat and what to eat is also key to maximizing performance .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; A slowing metabolism and gradual loss of muscle mass , estimated to be six to eight per cent per decade after the age of 30 , are two markers of aging that impact performance and nutritional needs .
Optimizing the diet of master athletes so as to slow down the physiological changes that occur as the decades add up is an important strategy when it comes to sustaining the volume and intensity needed to maximize potential .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;ldquo ; Master athletes who are able to maintain a high training volume and sufficient energy intake with age could maintain their body composition , metabolism and ultimately , resting metabolic rate ( the amount of energy expended at rest and during the activities of everyday life ) , &amp;rdquo ; said the research team .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; To assist in meeting these goals , master athletes need to consume more protein than younger athletes and their sedentary age-matched peers .
The current recommendation for older adults is 30 grams of protein per meal , 10 grams more than recommended for younger adults .
For master athletes however , 35-40 grams of protein at four-hour intervals throughout the day is considered crucial to repair and rebuild muscles utilized during exercise .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;ldquo ; Practically , this recommendation corresponds to a minimum of four portions of &amp;gt ; 30g proteins per day , for breakfast ( 8 a .
) , lunch ( 12 p .
) , afternoon snack ( 4 p .
) and dinner ( 8 p .
) for a total of around 120 g protein or 1 .
g/kg body mass per day for an 80-kg athlete , &amp;rdquo ; said the French researchers .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; In addition , a protein-rich snack should be consumed immediately post-exercise ( within the first 60 minutes ) for master athletes with high training loads or after an intense workout .
A pre-bedtime glass of milk will also aid in muscle recovery &amp;mdash ; especially after a tough day at the gym .
Any source of protein , animal or plant-based will do the trick , though there is some suggestion that protein-rich dairy products may be some of the best options .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; How effective are those extra few grams of protein ? One study of master athletes noted a 33- to 38-per-cent increase in muscle mass and strength among those who consistently consumed a high-protein post-weight-training snack compared to those who didn&amp;rsquo ; t .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Still , as attentive as master athletes are to their diet and training schedules , injury and short-term health issues are common .
A forced interruption from training and competition is a fact of life for athletes of all ages , but for master athletes even brief periods of inactivity can lead to a decrease in precious muscles mass .
Maintaining a protein-rich diet while on the mend can help minimize some of that loss .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; As for fat and carbohydrates , carbs should be periodized based on the volume of training with fewer carbs consumed on rest or easy days and greater amounts consumed pre , during and post workouts on days when training volume is high .
Fat should be ingested in moderate amounts with an emphasis on foods rich in anti-inflammatory omega-3 fatty acids , like nuts , avocados and fatty fish such as salmon and tuna .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Keep in mind that athletes should always rely on a food-first approach to realizing their dietary goals , versus consuming supplements in the form of powder , shakes , gels or pills .
There&amp;rsquo ; s no replacing the synergy of the macro and micronutrients found in food versus a manufactured product that often promises more than it delivers .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Also important to remember is that older athletes who limit themselves to moderate workouts of less than an hour , need nothing more than a healthy , protein rich diet to fuel their workouts .
But for master athletes with performance goals and a rigorous training and competition schedule , it&amp;rsquo ; s always wise to seek professional advice from a certified dietitian/sport nutrition specialist who can further individualize the special dietary needs of master athletes .

more of Jill Barker 's most recent fitness **28;43860;TOOLONG &lt;/ul&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;nbsp ; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;nbsp ; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;nbsp ; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;nbsp ; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;nbsp ; &lt;/p&gt; Jill Barker , Special to Montreal GazetteSun , 12 Jan 2020 11:00:26 **45;43890;TOOLONG &amp;amp ; FitnessHealthLifeLocal NewsScienceBrownstein : Diva Michelle Sweeney reveals the story of her abusive relationshiphttp : **28;43937;TOOLONG .

" alt= " Michelle Sweeney rehearses for her show , Her Songs , My Story , in Montreal , on Monday , Jan .

" data-portal-copyright= " Allen McInnis " **28;44002;TOOLONG " 1 " data-license-id= " 1689427 " /&gt; &lt;p&gt; Michelle Sweeney is rolling through a medley of Aretha Franklin favourites and manages to infuse light into what has been a rather bleak winter day .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Sweeney , unarguably one of the finest jazz and blues belters in this land , has that kind of power , be it in a sparse basement rehearsal hall or on the grandest of stages .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Sweeney is in a sparse Verdun basement studio at the moment , touching up her solo stage show , Her Songs , My Story , debuting Wednesday at Centaur Theatre&amp;rsquo ; s Wildside Festival .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; The songs are among the greatest covered by Aretha .
The story is decidedly Sweeney&amp;rsquo ; s .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; After rousing renderings of Think , Natural Woman and Respect , Sweeney takes a dramatic turn and begins recounting her voyage in this rehearsal : &amp;ldquo ; I&amp;rsquo ; ve been blessed with amazing opportunities in music , stage and film .
I have two loving children and am blessed by friends who believe in me .
For a long time , that has been my story .
&amp;rdquo ; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; And then she lets it all spill out : &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;ldquo ; Thirty years , 360 months , 1,560 weeks , 10,950 days , 262,800 hours , 15,768,000 minutes to wake up from the pain and a pillow filled with tears .
Thirty long years of living in fear of being discovered that someone finds out you&amp;rsquo ; re not as strong as they think &amp;hellip ; of wondering why you never felt love from the man you loved ; why you let him erase you by cheating , by beating you and leaving you for dead when he&amp;rsquo ; s through .
&amp;rdquo ; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Who knew ? Like so many others who have only recently spoken up about the physical and psychological abuse they had to endure in silence for years , precious few knew .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; This is a side of Sweeney that will leave fans and even longtime friends flabbergasted .
Best known for her bubbly stage presence , Sweeney will stun audiences with these revelations .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;ldquo ; No one really knew , &amp;rdquo ; Sweeney says during a rehearsal break .
&amp;ldquo ; I just smiled my way through it .
&amp;rdquo ; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; It was the death of Aretha in 2018 that somehow spurred Sweeney on to write this play .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;ldquo ; I wanted to pay tribute to her .
But I realized everyone was going to pay tribute , get up on stage to sing a couple of her songs .
So I decided to listen really closely to those songs , to dig deeply into the lyrics and see how they coincided with her life and my own .
That touched me to the core .
So I simply put my story together with her songs .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;ldquo ; I don&amp;rsquo ; t think this is what audiences are expecting .
But that&amp;rsquo ; s the reality .
I&amp;rsquo ; ve been telling the stories of others on stage for so long that I felt it was time for me to tell my own .
I was in an abusive relationship for years upon years .
I felt if I could tell my story , maybe it would help others come forward to say someone is doing something to them that must be stopped .
&amp;rdquo ; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Sweeney met Aretha only once , about 30 years ago , when the latter performed in Montreal .
Sweeney had spotted Aretha&amp;rsquo ; s tour bus outside a downtown hotel and planted herself in the hotel lobby for hours until she came down .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;ldquo ; We spent about four hours together , talking and shopping , &amp;rdquo ; Sweeney recalls .
&amp;ldquo ; I had two portraits made of her .
I gave her one on stage that night and she signed the other for me .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;ldquo ; I was a huge fan then as I am today .
When I heard the Queen of Soul died , I cried and cried , and began to reminisce about her life and the effect she had on my life .
&amp;rdquo ; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Not unlike Aretha , Sweeney began her musical career singing in gospel choirs in her hometown of Cleveland .
At 15 , she was already making a name for herself in local cabarets and performing on tour with Ronnie Love and the Drifters .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; When she was 20 , Sweeney was invited by Trevor Payne to join his famed Montreal Jubilation Gospel Choir .
She has stayed put in Montreal the last 35 years and become a staple on the jazz and blues scene here and throughout the country , performing with the likes of C&amp;eacute ; line Dion and Mary J .
Blige .
She stole the show in such local productions as Ain&amp;rsquo ; t Misbehavin&amp;rsquo ; and Eubie , and took on a slew of film and TV roles , sharing the screen with , among others , George Clooney and Wesley Snipes .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;ldquo ; I did a lot of laughing in public in those days , but people never know what many must go through in life and how hard it is to just keep it together on stage .
Now the secret is out .
Now people will know why I&amp;rsquo ; m always singing I Will Survive .

and Jan .

&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;ldquo ; I have a terminal illness , &amp;rdquo ; the retired federal civil servant says simply .
&amp;ldquo ; Pancreatic cancer .
&amp;rdquo ; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Plante still has enough energy to get dressed and venture outside with his son , but he knows that he will eventually have to seek &lt;a href= " https : **33;44380;TOOLONG .
care&lt;/a&gt; .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; And since late November , Plante has been preparing for that eventuality by visiting Montreal&amp;rsquo ; s first palliative day centre , located in C&amp;ocirc ; te-des-Neiges in what used to be the Church of St .

&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Despite the waning appetite that comes with cancer , Plante has enjoyed lunches prepared by a chef in a restaurant-grade kitchen at the day centre .

&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;ldquo ; Perfect ! &amp;rdquo ; he says , flashing an OK sign with his right hand .

Raphael Palliative Care Home and Day Centre opened in November after a $10-million fundraising campaign to finance the renovation and expansion of the greystone building that&amp;rsquo ; s nestled among tall pine trees .
Initially , though , some area residents were concerned that the centre might lead to an increase in the number of ambulances driving through the neighbourhood .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; But when the concept was explained to them during a public consultation , residents of the nearby Le Sanctuaire condo complex responded by donating furniture to the 12-bed home .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;ldquo ; It was important to have the community buy into this , &amp;rdquo ; said Marco Ottoni , vice-president of the home&amp;rsquo ; s board of directors .

Word spread quickly that a new palliative-care facility would open soon in the heart of the city , based on the concept that small is beautiful , that the terminally ill are entitled to the finest and most dignified care .
All its services would be free .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Within a matter of months , St .

After practising palliative medicine for 20 years at the MUHC , she joined St .
Raphael&amp;rsquo ; s as its medical director .
Lawlor began her career at the former Royal Victoria Hospital training under Balfour Mount , considered the father of palliative care in North America .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; But Lawlor had grown weary of &amp;ldquo ; swimming upstream&amp;rdquo ; in a large hospital setting that prizes &amp;ldquo ; prolonging life at all costs .
&amp;rdquo ; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;ldquo ; Hospitals are not designed for dying well , &amp;rdquo ; she said .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; At St .
Raphael&amp;rsquo ; s , it&amp;rsquo ; s hard to tell the difference between the guests of the day centre and the staff and volunteers .
No one wears a uniform .
During lunch , the staff eat at tables with the patients and guests .

" data-portal-copyright= " Dave Sidaway " **28;44647;TOOLONG " 1 " data-license-id= " 1666906 " /&gt; &lt;p&gt; A newly built atrium ensures that the building is awash in natural light all day long .
The non-profit centre plans to hold vernissages in the atrium to raise funds , connecting the community with those spending their final days within its walls .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; One of those patients was 71-year-old &lt;span dir= " auto " &gt;Nicole L'Archev ? que&lt;/span&gt; , who had lung cancer .
On an early December afternoon , L&amp;rsquo ; Archev&amp;ecirc ; que sat in her bedroom eating yogurt after being given a therapeutic sponge bath by a nurse .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;ldquo ; They are so tender , &amp;rdquo ; she said of the staff .
&amp;ldquo ; They give me hugs .
&amp;rdquo ; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; She peered out a large window at the snow-covered street .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;ldquo ; They say I have three and a half months , &amp;rdquo ; &lt;span dir= " auto " &gt;L'Archev ? que&lt;/span&gt; added .
&amp;ldquo ; But you never know .
You can&amp;rsquo ; t predict the future .
&amp;rdquo ; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &lt;span dir= " auto " &gt;Unfortunately , L'Archev ? que would not get to see the new year .
She died on Dec .
&lt;/span&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Palliative care is not just about easing pain and symptom management .
It&amp;rsquo ; s also about preparing for death .
To that end , patients are encouraged to produce legacy art and to make music and voice recordings .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Anne Lacourse , the music therapist , recalled how a young mother who was dying decided to record something for her children .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;ldquo ; In the recording , she tells her children what to do when they reach a certain age , &amp;rdquo ; Lacourse said .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; And when words are hard to come by , it&amp;rsquo ; s the music that soothes their agony and that can help reconcile a son or daughter who might be estranged from a parent .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;ldquo ; The music goes very quickly to the heart , &amp;rdquo ; she noted .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;img src= " https : **33;44677;TOOLONG .

&lt;br&gt;&lt;/span&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &lt;span class= " st " &gt;Touch is so important to the terminally ill , Jobin said , insisting that patients should not be deprived of physical affection in the last days of their lives .
&lt;/span&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Naturally , such care is expensive .

Raphael&amp;rsquo ; s $3 .
annual operating budget , but fundraising must cover the rest .

&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;ldquo ; For them , &amp;rdquo ; he said , &amp;ldquo ; it&amp;rsquo ; s a calling .

&lt;/p&gt; Aaron Derfel , Montreal GazetteMon , 06 Jan 2020 23:02:55 **45;44863;TOOLONG .
NewsFitness : Is stretching a waste of time ? http : **35;44910;TOOLONG .
&lt;img src= " https : **33;44947;TOOLONG .
title= " Ryan Poehling leads stretching exercises at a Laval Rocket practice in October .
Gymnasts , hockey players and swimmers all require different levels of flexibility .
" alt= " Ryan Poehling leads stretching exercises at a Laval Rocket practice in October .
Gymnasts , hockey players and swimmers all require different levels of flexibility .
" data-portal-copyright= " Dave Sidaway " **28;44982;TOOLONG " 1 " data-license-id= " 1684498 " /&gt; &lt;p&gt; The last time I wrote a controversial column about stretching , I got a record number of readers questioning the rationale behind eliminating stretching before a workout .
That was 20 years ago , when stretching was an integral part of almost all warmups .
Nowadays , not only has stretching disappeared from most pre-workout routines , American exercise scientist James Nuzzo is recommending removing stretching as one of the foundational pillars of physical fitness .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Nuzzo doesn&amp;rsquo ; t believe stretching is irrelevant .
He just wonders why trainers still prescribe stretching exercises for healthy individuals who want to improve their overall fitness , and why evaluating flexibility is still part of the curriculum of fitness tests delivered in schools and fitness clubs .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; To be clear , the type of stretching in question is static stretching , which requires holding stretches for 10 to 30 seconds .
Dynamic stretching , also called range of motion exercises , are movement-based and don&amp;rsquo ; t require any one position to be held for any length of time .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;ldquo ; Static stretching does not clearly and consistently improve health and function , &amp;rdquo ; Nuzzo said in a &lt;a href= " https : **33;45012;TOOLONG .
target= " blank " rel= " noopener " &gt;recent online edition of Sports Medicine&lt;/a&gt; .
&amp;ldquo ; Moreover , flexibility can be maintained or improved by exercise modalities that cause more robust health benefits than stretching ( e .
resistance training ) .
&amp;rdquo ; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Stretching was once heralded as an important element in preventing sports injuries and post-exercise soreness , but many of its fitness and health benefits have been debunked .
Current &lt;a href= " http : **33;45047;TOOLONG .
target= " blank " rel= " noopener " &gt;Canadian&lt;/a&gt; and &lt;a href= " https : **33;45082;TOOLONG .
target= " blank " rel= " noopener " &gt;American&lt;/a&gt; exercise guidelines make no mention of stretching in their recommendations for pursuing a healthy , active lifestyle .
Yet assessing flexibility still remains part of most fitness testing protocols , and the American College of Sports Medicine still recommends stretching all major muscle groups two to three days a week , claiming &amp;ldquo ; flexibility training will help to improve balance and postural stability .
&amp;rdquo ; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Flexibility testing is done using the sit-and-reach test , which entails sitting on the floor with both legs extended out in front of the body and reaching toward the toes .
Flexibility is assessed based on how far the fingers can extend toward the toes .
A single measure of flexibility , the sit-and-reach test evaluates range of motion in the hamstrings and lower back .
Since flexibility differs from joint to joint , it&amp;rsquo ; s possible to demonstrate a lack of mobility through the hips , hamstrings and lower back but still score in the upper percentiles for flexibility through the shoulders or ankles .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Nuzzo performed a scientific review to see if acing the sit-and-reach test has any health or functional benefits , including fewer injuries , reduced risk of falls among the elderly , a longer life , superior athletic performance , improved aerobic capacity , muscular strength or body composition or a better quality of life .
It turns out that whether flexibility is great , good or mediocre , there is little impact on any of these measures of health and fitness .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; In fact , when it comes to static stretching , there are plenty of reasons to be cautious .
Stretching temporarily reduces the amount of power the muscles can deliver , thereby reducing overall gains in speed , strength and power .
But Nuzzo says there&amp;rsquo ; s another good reason to forget about prescribing stretching as part of a general fitness program : it&amp;rsquo ; s a waste of time .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;ldquo ; Time previously dedicated to stretching can be reallocated to activities that cause more robust health benefits , including improved flexibility , &amp;rdquo ; said Nuzzo .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Strength training exercises that move a joint through its full range of motion can improve flexibility .
In fact , studies have shown weight training has the potential to increase sit-and-reach scores by 10 to 25 per cent .
Aerobic exercise boosted sit-and-reach scores by 10 to 17 per cent .
While those scores are lower than the improvements in flexibility gained through static stretching ( nine to 43 per cent ) , they&amp;rsquo ; re in the ballpark .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Keep in mind that greater flexibility isn&amp;rsquo ; t always a goal worth pursuing .
Joint hypermobility has been associated with joint pain and a greater risk of injury .
A healthy joint is strong and flexible enough to perform sport-specific movements with efficiency and power .
That means gymnasts , hockey players and swimmers all require different levels of flexibility .
The same goes for a hockey goalie , kicker in football and martial arts aficionado .
Each sport has its own requirements when it comes to what kind of stretching delivers the best possible performance with the lowest risk of injury .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; So , should you stretch or not ? The choice is yours .
If your yoga class makes it easier for you to get in and out of a squat , bend over to pick something up off the floor or skate from end to end during your beer league hockey game , then stick with it .
Or if your physiotherapist suggests improving flexibility or range of motion in order to improve movement patterns or fend off specific aches and pains , go for it .
For everyone else who is otherwise healthy but feels guilty about avoiding stretching , consider this a hall pass .

&lt;ul class= " relatedlinks " &gt; &lt;li&gt;&lt;a href= " https : **33;45159;TOOLONG .
five fitness resolutions are easy to **25;45194;TOOLONG &lt;li&gt;&lt;a href= " https : **33;45221;TOOLONG .
go the distance to get a Peloton .

from Jill **27;45291;TOOLONG &lt;/ul&gt; Jill Barker , Special to Montreal GazetteSun , 05 Jan 2020 16:25:00 **45;45320;TOOLONG &amp;amp ; FitnessBrownstein : Are you game enough to try the hemp burger ? http : **33;45367;TOOLONG .
&lt;img src= " https : **33;45402;TOOLONG .
title= " Ezra Soiferman , a Montreal filmmaker and hemp enthusiast , prepares to dig into a hemp-based burger as Hello 123 co-owner Eric Blake looks on .
" alt= " Ezra Soiferman , a Montreal filmmaker and hemp enthusiast , prepares to dig into a hemp-based burger as Hello 123 co-owner Eric Blake looks on .
" data-portal-copyright= " Pierre Obendrauf " **28;45437;TOOLONG " 1 " data-license-id= " 1662696 " /&gt; &lt;p&gt; Where&amp;rsquo ; s the buzz ? &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; It&amp;rsquo ; s in the flavour , grasshopper .
Believe it .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; We&amp;rsquo ; re talking burgers and burritos , among other munchies , infused with hemp at Hello 123 , a vegan brasserie in **26;45467;TOOLONG ; ce .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; As anyone who has ever attempted to smoke or eat it in search of a buzz , hemp &amp;mdash ; although derived from cannabis like marijuana &amp;mdash ; does not contain the necessary THC content of the latter to get one high .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Hemp , evidently the first crop ever cultivated by humankind 10,000 years ago , is primarily known for its industrial use in everything from rope to paper , beauty products to clothing .
But food ? &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; And so it is that a vegetarian , Gazette photographer Pierre Obendrauf , and an unrepentant carnivore , yours truly , have descended upon Hello 123 with a dollop , bordering on gusts , of skepticism in sampling some of the dozen hemp-laden items on the menu .
We console ourselves with the fact we can take relief , if necessary , from the fully loaded booze bar .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; But no gagging here as we bite into the Ezra Burger , a hemp/sunflower patty with pickles , sweet onions , Boston lettuce , tomato , toasted hemp hearts and the Ez Sez Secret Sauce .
It is to die for , save that it won&amp;rsquo ; t kill you .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Unlike those &lt;a href= " https : **33;45495;TOOLONG .
target= " blank " rel= " noopener " &gt;plant-based burgers that seek to replicate the beef flavour&lt;/a&gt; , this one doesn&amp;rsquo ; t at all , tasting a lot more like falafel , except it contains none .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;ldquo ; It&amp;rsquo ; s not dry as one might expect , &amp;rdquo ; Obendrauf says .
&amp;ldquo ; And it doesn&amp;rsquo ; t fall apart .
&amp;rdquo ; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;img src= " https : **33;45530;TOOLONG .
title= " Co-owner Eric Blake pours hemp seeds at Hello 123 .
" alt= " Co-owner Eric Blake pours hemp seeds at Hello 123 .
" data-portal-copyright= " Pierre Obendrauf " **28;45565;TOOLONG " 1 " data-license-id= " 1662700 " /&gt; &lt;p&gt; Obendrauf&amp;rsquo ; s only issue is that he could have done without the pickles .
Mine is that neither Hello 123 co-owner Eric Blake or filmmaker Ezra Soiferman , for whom the Ezra Burger is named , will reveal the contents of the secret sauce &amp;mdash ; although they insist it&amp;rsquo ; s all above board .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Obendrauf is even more blown away with the Cauliflower Tahini with Hemp and Sunflower Balls , with , among other ingredients , salsa , pomegranate , quinoa and sesame , served with lemon tahini and chimichurri sauces .
&amp;ldquo ; The sunflower brings everything out , &amp;rdquo ; Obendrauf marvels .
&amp;ldquo ; An entirely new food sensation for me .
&amp;rdquo ; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; We&amp;rsquo ; re both bullish on the Superfood Burrito Bowl , filled with kale , guacamole , cashew cream and hemp seeds .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Then it&amp;rsquo ; s on to the unique Hello 123 Caesar Salad , which packs coconut bacon , oat-seed crackers , tamari almonds and hemp seeds .
But which , unlike most Caesar salads , won&amp;rsquo ; t have loved ones and colleagues dashing away from you due to high levels of garlic emanating from your breath .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; No shortage of hemp-filled brunch and desert items , either : pancakes , waffles , banana French toast , Blue Smoothie Bowl and &amp;hellip ; mmm &amp;hellip ; &amp;nbsp ; an avocado chocolate mousse , also to die for .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; The N .
Hello 123 , open since June , has a sister operation , H123 in St-Henri , and two Kupfert &amp;amp ; Kim cousins in the city .
There are also two Hello 123 locations in Toronto .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;ldquo ; The whole idea about introducing hemp to our menus is that it is so high in protein , fibre and nutritional benefits , &amp;rdquo ; Blake says .
&amp;ldquo ; The hemp seed , while not having a distinctive smell , has a bit of a crunch to it .
It&amp;rsquo ; s just a matter of integrating it with the other ingredients to bring out all the flavours .
&amp;rdquo ; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; It&amp;rsquo ; s not just the contents of the food that are striking .
It&amp;rsquo ; s also the presentation .
The colours and composition of each plate hold up with the grandest of those in haute cuisine salons .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;ldquo ; There had been this misconception in some quarters that vegan is not very sexy , &amp;rdquo ; Blake says .
&amp;ldquo ; But that&amp;rsquo ; s changing a lot now these days with social media .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;ldquo ; Ten to 15 years ago , many people assumed vegans ate only salads and nuts , but &lt;a href= " https : **33;45595;TOOLONG .
target= " blank " rel= " noopener " &gt;things have really evolved a lot over the last few years on the vegan front&lt;/a&gt; .
This is wholesome fare that holds its own with any tasty food out there .
&amp;rdquo ; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;img src= " https : **33;45630;TOOLONG .
title= " It 's not just the contents of the food that are striking ; it 's also the presentation , writes Bill Brownstein .
" alt= " It 's not just the contents of the food that are striking ; it 's also the presentation , writes Bill Brownstein .
" data-portal-copyright= " Pierre Obendrauf " **28;45665;TOOLONG " 1 " data-license-id= " 1662703 " /&gt; &lt;p&gt; Blake recalls trying to talk his father into sampling his food .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;ldquo ; Like so many others , he had no understanding of what &lt;a href= " https : **33;45695;TOOLONG .
target= " blank " rel= " noopener " &gt;vegan food&lt;/a&gt; was , and he simply frowned and told me he would prefer some steak instead when I asked him to give it a try , &amp;rdquo ; Blake says .

&amp;ldquo ; I&amp;rsquo ; m hemp to toe , and eating it , too .
&amp;rdquo ; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Indeed , another kind of high .

BusinessLocal Food ReviewsLocal NewsBrownstein : What irks letter-writers to the mayor ? A furry animalhttp : **34;45914;TOOLONG .
&lt;img src= " https : **33;45950;TOOLONG .
title= " Montrealers , particularly in the Ahuntsic -- Cartierville borough , which has had the highest number of issues , have reason to be alarmed about coyotes .
" alt= " Montrealers , particularly in the Ahuntsic -- Cartierville borough , which has had the highest number of issues , have reason to be alarmed about coyotes .
" data-portal-copyright= " John Mahoney " **28;45985;TOOLONG " 1 " data-license-id= " 1413760 " /&gt; &lt;iframe width= " 100% " height= " 100% " frameborder= " 0 " allowfullscreen= " true " src= " https : **34;46015;TOOLONG .
&gt; &lt;/iframe&gt; &lt;p&gt; Montreal Mayor Val&amp;eacute ; rie Plante gets mail .
Lots and lots of mail .
About 35,000 pieces over 2018 and 2019 until the end of November .
Most are emails , with a sprinkling of snail mail .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; But few could possibly guess what leaves the mayor&amp;rsquo ; s letter-writers most in a dander .
Hint : it&amp;rsquo ; s not two-legged life-forms , and it&amp;rsquo ; s not two- or four-wheeled vehicles .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Naturally , one might expect the bulk of the correspondence would deal with such citizen beefs as construction , traffic , public transit , parking , snow removal , sidewalks , bike lanes , &amp;nbsp ; Airbnbs , Camillien-Houde , cal&amp;egrave ; ches , the postponing of Halloween , shutting down of the Jeanne-Mance Park north softball field , Bill 21 and , oh yeah , the budget .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Not even close .
Far and away , the topic that appears to have left Montrealers howling the most over this two-year period has been &amp;hellip ; coyotes ? &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Yup .
Nearly 2,400 have communicated their feelings on coyotes to the mayor .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Compare that with the mere 353 who had budget concerns in 2018 .
Or how about that hot-button issue of the Camillien-Houde thoroughfare ? Only 292 expressed their views there .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Surely , the ever-slippery issue of snow removal must really resonate .
Not as much as some of us skeptics would imagine .
Just 400 sounded off .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; But there must have been an uproar over the mayor&amp;rsquo ; s &lt;a href= " http : **34;46051;TOOLONG .
target= " blank " rel= " noopener " &gt;suggestion to move Halloween to the following night&lt;/a&gt; .
Yeah , right .
All of 35 people registered their outrage .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; There&amp;rsquo ; s no way that the sudden and arbitrary closure of the &lt;a href= " http : **34;46087;TOOLONG .
target= " blank " rel= " noopener " &gt;Jeanne-Mance Park softball field&lt;/a&gt; &amp;mdash ; where there was no public consultation &amp;mdash ; didn&amp;rsquo ; t bring out brickbats by the score .
Would you believe that only a handful bothered to write the mayor and register their displeasure ? But such was the case .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Given the reaction to coyotes , one would have every reason to suspect that the subject of &lt;a href= " http : **34;46123;TOOLONG .
target= " blank " rel= " noopener " &gt;now-banned cal ? ches&lt;/a&gt; would certainly provoke much heated reaction one way or another .
Not really .
Only about 150 writers have made their opinions known on this front .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; After coyotes , &amp;nbsp ; the next highest grouping of correspondences dealt with the Technoparc ( 1,248 ) and a zero-waste contest ( 752 ) .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; As for the coyotes , residents , particularly in the Ahuntsic&amp;ndash ; Cartierville borough , which has had the highest number of issues , &lt;a href= " https : **33;46159;TOOLONG .
target= " blank " rel= " noopener " &gt;have reason to be alarmed&lt;/a&gt; .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; In the summer of 2018 , there were an inordinate number of coyote sightings and three attacks on young children in the area .
The city sent out teams to attempt to shoo the coyotes away from certain areas .
The city also advised residents to keep a lid on food waste and not to feed or get chummy with the critters .
But what probably led to the ire of some citizens and animal-rights activists was the plan to euthanize overly aggressive coyotes .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Unbeknownst to many , coyotes have called the island of Montreal home since the early 1970s , and efforts to relocate and/or eradicate them have been mostly unsuccessful .
&amp;nbsp ; Since 2017 , there have been around 1,000 sightings and about two dozen incidents of attacks on humans .
The city set up a coyote hotline to deal with the dilemma , but has come to terms with the fact that coyotes are part of our biodiversity .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Jimmy Zoubris , special adviser to Plante , is impressed that about 35,000 citizens took the time to go to the city website to track down the mayor&amp;rsquo ; s email and snail-mail addresses .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;ldquo ; There is a real commitment here , &amp;rdquo ; Zoubris says .
&amp;ldquo ; It&amp;rsquo ; s not like just going to Facebook or Twitter .
It&amp;rsquo ; s people who took the time to sign in and send a message .
&amp;rdquo ; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Zoubris is also shocked by some of the results .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;ldquo ; People always have strong opinions when it comes to animals .
So it&amp;rsquo ; s understandable the issue of coyotes would touch a nerve for many , especially those who live by the river where the coyotes often roam , &amp;rdquo ; Zoubris says .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &amp;ldquo ; But you&amp;rsquo ; d think other issues , like the budget .
Or Airbnbs , &lt;a href= " http : **34;46194;TOOLONG .
target= " blank " rel= " noopener " &gt;which is a huge issue in the Plateau , &lt;/a&gt; only drew nine letters .
Or bilingualism , in the sense that some think the mayor is speaking too much English , would draw a lot of mail , particularly with Bill 21 in the spotlight , but only 55 commented on this .
&amp;rdquo ; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; And in a city where drivers lament they can&amp;rsquo ; t get there from here or there because of all the construction and detours , would you believe only 42 expressed their displeasure on the subject of traffic over the first 11 months of this year ? &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Incidentally , all the writers get a response , occasionally from the mayor but most times from the departmental official responsible for the particular issue .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Though they might not be well represented on the mail front , Zoubris does point out that citizens have expressed themselves , often rather vociferously , on Facebook and Twitter when it comes to cal&amp;egrave ; ches , Camillien-Houde and the softball field .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; As anyone in the world of politics can attest , few ever write to express their admiration for the person in office .
Even still , it&amp;rsquo ; s somewhat astonishing that Plante&amp;rsquo ; s office has received only 21 notifications of &amp;ldquo ; bons mots&amp;rdquo ; &amp;mdash ; good sentiments in no particular area on a job well done &amp;mdash ; this year .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Don&amp;rsquo ; t know if Mayor Plante can count on getting more &amp;ldquo ; bons mots&amp;rdquo ; for the coming year , but she had better brace herself for plenty of feedback in a couple of other areas , such as her insistence on proposing the naming of an REM station after Bernard Landry .
In November alone , she had already received 300 reactions .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; And then there&amp;rsquo ; s the issue that just never goes away : &lt;a href= " http : **34;46230;TOOLONG .
target= " blank " rel= " noopener " &gt;Camillien-Houde Way&lt;/a&gt; .
Wild guess : talk about possibly turning it into a one-way thoroughfare , among other schemes , &amp;nbsp ; could trigger a tsunami of mail .
&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Or not .
